 The English models Verb Can and Could are used quite a lot when speaking and writing
 vaakya frem main sahi jagah iskaa upyog kiya jaae isliye niyamon kaa jaananaa jaruri he
 Know where is the use of Can and Could and what is the difference between these two? 1
 kisi baat kii sambhaavna hone par(a)can kaa prayog ham Present Tense ke liye karte hai
 Can is used for what is possible at the moment
 example:you can easily walk in moonlight
 (b) At the same time, Could is used for Past tense
 example:you Could Easily walk in Moonlight
 (c) Could is also used for the future but it is not fixed
 example:if you don't hurry you could be late
 (it may or may not be late here) 2
 kisi kii ijaajat leni ho yaa deni ho to(a)ham kisi se koi kaam karne kii ijaajat lene or dene ke liye Can kaa prayog karte hai
 Example: Can i do this job, Please? You can go home now if you like
 (b)haalanki aisi sthiti main Could kaprayog karnaa zyada behtarhoga kyonki isse aapaki shishtataa kaa pataa chalata he
 Example: Could i do this work, Please? You could go your home3
 nivedan or nirdesh ke liye(a)agar ham kisi se madad lete hai yaa koi kaam karne ke liye kehete hai to usamen bhi Can kaa prayog karte hai
 Example: Can i use your Phone, Please? Can i have my Water Bill, Please? (B) It would be better if we use Could while asking for help
 aise vaakyon ko Could se shuru karnaa aapke achche vyavhaar ko batayega
 Example: Could i use your Phone, Please? Could i have my Water Bill, Please? 4
 yogyata bataane ke liye(a)kisi kii skills ko bataane ke liye Can kaa prayog kiya jaataa he
 Example: She can sing a classical song
 (b)vahiin, yogyata ke sandarbh main Could kaa prayog kisi ke Past kobatane ke liekia jaataa he
 Example: He Could Run Like a leopardshe Could Sing a Classical song
 5
 If you want to offer something, we can use Can to make something
 example:can i do this if You like? The doors of paradise need fresh paint

 agar muslimon kii baat karen to sirf 10% muslimon ne bijepi gathbandhan ko vot kiya, jabaki 87% muslimon ne congress ko or 3% ne anya ko vot diya

 savarna matadaataaon main se 78% ne bijepi gathbandhan ko, 16% ne congress ko or 6% ne anya ko vot diya
 According to surveys by India Today and Axis My India, 75% of OBC and Rajput voters voted for the BJP alliance, while only 20% of OBC and 19% of Rajput voters voted for the Congress
 5,000 rupee se kam masik kharch vaale pariwaron kii baat karen, to is varg ke 62% matadaataaon ne bijepi or 34% matadaataaon ne congress ko vot diya

 ' mazdooron ko hadtaal se rokane ke liye vitt mantri arun jetali, petroleum mantri dharmendra pradhan or shram mantri bandaaru dattatreya ne sabhi unionon ke netaaon ke saath baithak kii
 But trade unions are angry over several important issues related to changes in labor laws
 majdoor sanghathanon kii sabase badi shikaayat he ki kanoonon main badlaav ko lekar unki raay nahin lee gai
 Because of these changes, it will be easy to get workers fired
 yahi nahin, mazdooron kii buniyadi suraksha bhi kaaphi kamjor pad jaaegi
